## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 Header Normalization Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that handle HTTP/1.1 to HTTP/2 header translation: the header case normalization (lowercase), the pseudo-header injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority), and the upgrade header handling.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Files for HTTP/1.1 → HTTP/2 Header Translation

### 1. Header Case Normalization (Lowercase)
- **`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`** — `ConnectionImpl::completeCurrentHeader()`: Applies `absl::ascii_tolower` to every HTTP/1.1 header field name as it's parsed, normalizing to lowercase.
- **`source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc`** — `ProperCaseHeaderKeyFormatter::format()`: Optional Title-Case formatter for HTTP/1.1 output.

### 2. Pseudo-header Injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority)
- **`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`**:
  - `ServerConnectionImpl::handlePath()`: Injects `:path`, `:scheme`, `:authority` from the HTTP/1.1 request-line/Host header
  - `ServerConnectionImpl::onHeadersCompleteBase()`: Injects `:method`
- **`source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc`** — `mutateRequestHeaders()`: Sets `:scheme` from `x-forwarded-proto` or TLS state when absent

### 3. Upgrade Header Handling
- **`source/common/http/utility.cc`** / **`utility.h`**: Core transform functions — `transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2`, `transformUpgradeRequestFromH2toH1`, `transformUpgradeResponseFromH1toH2`, `transformUpgradeResponseFromH2toH1`
- **`source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc`**: Uses the transforms in `ClientStreamImpl::encodeHeaders()` (H1→H2 upgrade) and `ServerStreamImpl::decodeHeaders()` (H2→H1 conversion)
- **`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc`**: UHV layer performs the same transforms for `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator` and `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator`

Pseudo-header Injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority)\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc`**:\\n- `ServerConnectionImpl::onHeadersCompleteBase()` (line 1218): injects `:method` via `headers->setMethod(parser_->methodName())`\\n- `ServerConnectionImpl::handlePath()` (line 1100-1163): injects `:path`, `:scheme` (via `headers.setScheme(absl::AsciiStrToLower(absolute_url.scheme()))`), and `:authority` (via `headers.setHost(absolute_url.hostAndPort())`) from the HTTP/1.1 request line for absolute-form URLs\\n\\n**`source/common/http/conn_manager_utility.cc`** \u2014 `ConnectionManagerUtility::mutateRequestHeaders()` (~line 205): Sets `:scheme` pseudo-header from `x-forwarded-proto` when not already present, or based on TLS state.\\n\\n## 3. Upgrade Header Handling (HTTP/1.1 Upgrade <-> HTTP/2 Extended CONNECT)\\n\\n**`source/common/http/utility.cc`** and **`source/common/http/utility.h`**:\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()`: Converts HTTP/1.1 Upgrade to H2 extended CONNECT \u2014 sets `:method: CONNECT`, moves `Upgrade` to `:protocol`, removes `Connection`/`Upgrade` headers.\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH3()`: Delegates to H2 transform.\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeResponseFromH1toH2()`: Converts HTTP/1.1 101 to HTTP/2 200.\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeRequestFromH2toH1()`: Reverse \u2014 extended CONNECT back to HTTP/1.1 Upgrade.\\n- `Utility::transformUpgradeResponseFromH2toH1()`: Converts HTTP/2 200 back to HTTP/1.1 101.\\n\\n**`source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc`**:\\n- `ConnectionImpl::ClientStreamImpl::encodeHeaders()`: When encoding upgrade requests for H2 upstream, calls `transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2`.\\n- `ConnectionImpl::ServerStreamImpl::encodeHeaders()`: When encoding upgrade responses for H2, calls `transformUpgradeResponseFromH1toH2`.\\n- `ConnectionImpl::ServerStreamImpl::decodeHeaders()`: When decoding incoming H2 extended CONNECT, calls `transformUpgradeRequestFromH2toH1` to present as H/1 upgrade to upper layers.\\n\\n**`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc`** (UHV layer):\\n- `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders()`: Converts H2 extended CONNECT to H/1 upgrade.\\n- `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders()`: Converts H/1 upgrade to H2 extended CONNECT for upstream.\\n- `ServerHttp2HeaderValidator::transformResponseHeaders()`: Converts H/1 upgrade response to H2 extended CONNECT response.\\n- `ClientHttp2HeaderValidator::transformResponseHeaders()`: Converts H2 extended CONNECT response back to H/1 upgrade response.\\n\\n**`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http1_header_validator.cc`**: HTTP/1.1-specific header validation including pseudo-header checking.\\n\\nThe complete pipeline:\\n1. HTTP/1.1 parser receives headers \u2192 `completeCurrentHeader()` lowercases field names\\n2. `handlePath()` injects `:path`, `:scheme`, `:authority` from the request line\\n3. `onHeadersCompleteBase()` injects `:method`\\n4. `mutateRequestHeaders()` in conn_manager_utility sets `:scheme` if still missing\\n5. When forwarding to H2 upstream with Upgrade: `encodeHeaders()` calls `transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2()`\\n6. On response path: `transformUpgradeResponseFromH2toH1()` restores HTTP/1.1 101 format\"\n}\n",
